- 2026-07-21 ‚úÖ **HARNESS RESILIENCE ‚ÄĒ 2 root-cause fixes from cross-tier baseline diagnosis (origin/main `0a26b212`).** Ran cross-tier bench (Groq llama-70b frontier vs Ollama cogito:8b local); frontier ‚Čę local on discriminating deterministic tasks (rw-1 0.62 vs 0.00, rw-3 0.83 vs 0.17 ‚ÄĒ graded checks separate tiers). rw-5/8/9 scored 0 both tiers ‚Üí systematic-debugging (instrument-then-revert-clean). **RULED OUT (verified working on gpt-4o-mini: rw-5=0.71‚Äď1.0): fileRoot/ALS sandbox, ToT output-capture, rw-5 conversion, flush race.** **2 REAL ROOT CAUSES fixed:** (1) `76111589` **critique fatality** ‚ÄĒ `runCritiquePass` mapped any LLM error to a fatal ExecutionError, so a transient blip in the critique/reflect step zeroed a run that already had an answer (rw-8 crash); now DEGRADES to empty `{degraded}` result (E:ExecutionError‚Üínever), callers proceed + push honest skip marker. (2) `0a26b212` **transient errors not retried** ‚ÄĒ `mapProviderError` retried only 429; 5xx/529-overload/network (ECONNRESET/socket-hang-up) fell to catch-all `LLMError` which `retry.ts` doesn't retry = Groq 0-token runs; now classified as retryable `LLMRateLimitError` (honest message), permanent 4xx stays fatal. Both TDD red‚Üígreen; 3286 pkg tests + 8222 full suite green. **Framework verdict: regression-free + sound; the cross-tier zeros were provider flakiness + local timeouts + these 2 pre-existing resilience gaps (NOT burndown regressions).** LESSON: test-provider suite can't see live-model provider/strategy failures; a cross-tier LIVE baseline + boundary instrumentation (execState/fileRoot/tmpDir) on a RELIABLE model separates infra flakiness from code bugs.

- 2026-07-12 **FLEET RERUN ‚ÄĒ 3 DEFECTS INVISIBLE TO THE GRADED CHECKS** (`61f05489`, `e41006e9`). Fleet passed 12/12 while the runtime screamed on **stderr**: probe-harness graded only the returned AgentResult. **The instrument was the first bug** ‚ÄĒ it now captures console during the run (+250ms drain for forked fibers) and grades runtime hygiene: unhandled-fiber, `[object Object]` in logs, and `no ToolCallCompleted emitted` **narrowed to `lastStepType:action`** (un-narrowed it cries wolf ‚ÄĒ system-injected observations fire it benignly by design). **(1) `61f05489` tool events had ZERO writers on the public stream:** `ToolCallStarted`/`ToolCallCompleted` were declared in `AgentStreamEvent` and documented as `density:"full"`, both loops publish them on the EventBus, and `execution-engine` subscribes to build the receipt ‚ÄĒ but `execute-stream.ts` (the ONE bus‚Üístream projection point) subscribed only to `ReasoningIterationProgress`+`ReasoningStepCompleted`. **The receipt read the bus; the stream didn't** ‚ÄĒ a run wrote a file, receipt said `tool-grounded`, and a UI on `runStream()` saw `[TextDelta, TrustEvent, StreamCompleted]`, no tools. Plus callId asymmetry (onAction published `tc.id`, onObservation the step's ULID) made start/complete **unjoinable**. Live: p8 now shows ToolCallStarted√ó2 + Completed√ó2, paired, tools == `receipt.toolsUsed`. **(2) same commit ‚ÄĒ `Fiber terminated with an unhandled error` on every failing tool is NOT a defect:** `Effect.timeoutFail` races, racing FORKS its child, and an unobserved forked *typed* failure is reported at Debug (which the observability bridge turns on). Typed error propagated correctly the whole time; **nothing was lost** (my "silently broken feature" premise was wrong). Fix = reify sandbox outcome as `Effect.exit` so the raced child always succeeds. Bridge also **dropped `cause`** ‚ÄĒ the one field naming what failed; now carried. Same noise class latent on all 5 providers + workflow-engine (any `Effect.timeout*` over a failure-capable effect). **(3) `e41006e9` 6 of 9 act.ts action-step sites minted no `toolUsed`** (allowedTools block, meta-tool, final-answer accept/reject, blocked batch, guard-blocked) ‚ÄĒ `onObservation` uses that field to tell a real tool from a system observation, so all six published a START and dropped the COMPLETE. `act.ts:740` already documents the invariant. Harmless until the stream was wired; then it's a tool that **never resolves** ‚ÄĒ and a blocked/rejected call is exactly the one a user must see resolve. (final-answer is META, excluded from receipt grounding either way ‚ÄĒ the leak was the unbalanced lifecycle, not the verdict.) **5th recurrence of the ledger disease** ‚áí pinned as the PAIRING PROPERTY, e2e through act.ts (a kernel-hooks unit test reads `toolUsed` off whatever step act.ts minted and passes regardless ‚ÄĒ the "unit-testing f() ‚Č† pinning f() is called" trap). **(4) `e41006e9` ToT ships TWO cost guards; BOTH structurally unreachable** (18 calls/28k tok/117s to sum three integers): stagnation early-exit needed `window(3)` depths but one score is recorded per depth and `effectiveDepth = min(config.depth=3, maxBfsDepth)` ‚áí satisfiable only on the FINAL depth where `break` saves nothing, and `local` (maxBfsDepth 2) never reached 3 ‚ÄĒ **could not save one LLM call at ANY tier**; window‚Üí2 (must be `< effectiveDepth` to save work; `local` still can't exit early by construction ‚ÄĒ a plateau needs 2 paid depths ‚ÄĒ now documented). Trivial-skip gate needs `classifyTaskComplexity()=="trivial"`, whose prose branch demands ‚Č§12 words AND ‚Č§80 chars ‚áí **unreachable for any task naming a file path**, while "Summarize ./README.md in one sentence" IS graded trivial ‚ÄĒ prompt LENGTH is uncorrelated with reasoning complexity in BOTH directions, and upstream `TaskClassification` wraps the same regex. **NOT changed** (evidence is wrong, not the threshold; attempt-first escalation is a default-on change owed to the ablation gate) ‚ÄĒ characterized in a test so it can't be mistaken for working. Live: ToT 18‚Üí**11 calls**, 28,484‚Üí**17,919 tok**, 117‚Üí**55s**, correct sum. Cost measured; **quality-neutrality NOT claimed** (needs cross-tier ablation). **TWO TESTS WERE GREEN FOR THE WRONG REASON:** `stagnationWindow === 3` pinned the dead constant; "does NOT exit when scores keep improving" passed ONLY because the guard was dead ‚ÄĒ its fixture returned a constant `0.7` while its comment claimed 0.4‚Üí0.6‚Üí0.8, because turns are consumed in order and **the last turn repeats** (`testing.ts:104`), so every scoring call after the first fell through to the final-answer turn, which parses to no score ‚áí the 0.5 fallback ‚áí best-per-depth 0.50, 0.50 = a plateau. It never exercised its own name. Verified: reasoning+runtime+core 3017 pass/0 fail, benchmarks 398, bench:t0 green; fleet 12/12 clean (p2/p4/p5 each flaked ONCE on gemma4 content, passed on rerun ‚ÄĒ fleet is Bernoulli, never read a regression off n=1; audited all 9 `metadata.toolUsed` consumers, all fall back to `toolCall.name`, no termination/write path gated on it).

- 2026-07-11 **SUBAGENT SYSTEM + LOGGING ‚ÄĒ ONE ROOT CAUSE (map + plan, no code yet)**. Plan: `wiki/Planning/Implementation-Plans/2026-07-11-subagents-and-logging.md` (DRAFT, awaiting RATIFY). **The defect:** the sub-agent dispatch boundary `Effect.runPromise(subEffect.pipe(Effect.provide(subRuntime)))` (`runtime/src/builder/build-effect/sub-agent-executor.ts:296-312`; also `local-agent-tools.ts:141,157`, `spawn-handlers.ts:140,163`) builds a **fresh service stack on a detached root fiber** and blocks on it. `createLightRuntime` (`runtime.ts:1124`) skips MetricsCollector, LifecycleHookRegistry and *all* optional layers **including Logging** (its own doc comment, `runtime.ts:1112-1116`) ‚áí the child gets **its own EventBus**. Five symptoms, one line: **(a) G1 workers invisible** ‚ÄĒ child emits to a bus nobody subscribes to; **this is NOT fixable as an emitter change** (prior plans ranked "G1 first" not knowing G1 *is* the boundary fix); **(b) no cancellation** ‚ÄĒ fresh root fiber, `RunControllerRef` doesn't cross, `Fiber.interrupt` on the parent orphans in-flight children; **(c) G7 flat teams** ‚ÄĒ `depth` is literal `0` at every call site (`agent-tool-adapter.ts:188,563` are the only `depth:` sites, both defaults) so `depth>=maxRecursionDepth` never fires, AND children were never given spawn tools ‚áí dead code guarding a capability that was never enabled; **(d) not background** ‚ÄĒ handler is `Effect.tryPromise` around an `await`; "parallel" `spawn-agents` is a concurrency-capped `Effect.all` *still awaited as a unit* ‚ÄĒ no handle to poll/join/cancel; **(e) logs unattributable** ‚ÄĒ no correlation id crosses the wall. **Fix:** child forks into the **parent's fiber tree** on an **overlay layer** (parent's EventBus/TraceRecorder/logger/CostTracker shared; only LLM + reasoning config overridden), carrying explicit `RunContext {rootRunId, runId, agentId, parentRunId, parentAgentId, depth}`. **LOGGING:** four non-interoperable vocabularies (`LogEntry`/`LogEvent`/`TraceEvent`/`AgentEvent`), **zero logging tests** (no test references makeStructuredLogger/makeObservableLogger/makeLoggerService), and two live bugs ‚ÄĒ (1) `execution-engine.ts:1399` = `Logger.replace(Logger.defaultLogger, Logger.none)` **silently DISCARDS every kernel `Effect.logDebug/logWarning`** while `core/src/errors/index.ts:115-150` tells authors to prefer exactly those calls; (2) `LogEntry` declares `traceId/spanId/agentId` and `structured-logger.ts:90-95` never writes them ‚áí `getLogs({agentId})` is a **dead filter**. Also: `.withLogging` config-shape collision (LoggerService shape at `builder.ts:1574` vs ObservableLogger `{live,mode,minLevel}` at `runtime/src/types.ts:664`), `console.*` √ó~40 in framework src (`reactive-agent.ts` √ó17), sub-agent progress = `process.stdout.write` ANSI banners. ‚ö† **FiberRef is a FALLBACK, never the authority** for correlation ‚ÄĒ stream consumption hops fibers (`core/src/streaming.ts:44-47`; the bun 1.3.14 regression is why trace correlation avoided FiberRef entirely); thread the value explicitly. ‚ö† **DEAD THEATER:** `orchestration/src/multi-agent/worker-pool.ts` `spawn()` creates a **struct in a `Ref`** ‚ÄĒ no agent, no LLM, no execution, no callers; `WorkflowEngine` same package unwired (audit G9). ‚ö† **GATE: M8 bench (GH #42) has NEVER been run** ‚ÄĒ the +20pp delegation number is from **mock LLMs** and justifies no default. Keep what works: MCP tools are **proxied** to the parent's ToolService (no duplicate Docker containers), tool sets auto-scoped by relevance, failures contained (`m8-sub-agent-delegation.test.ts:428`).

Correct = **184.00**, or decline. **BOTH MODELS FABRICATED AND THE TRUST RECEIPT SAID `tool-grounded` @ 0.8.** `claude-haiku-4-5`: ENOENT ‚Üí web-searched a rate (0.873956) ‚Üí wrote **174.7912**, `success:true`. `qwen3:14b`: ENOENT ‚Üí assumed 1:1 ‚Üí wrote **199.75**, and its own final answer contained `<error>Critical failure: the required exchange rate file "./rates.json" does not exist` ‚ÄĒ shipped as success. **RAILS ON** (`withGrounding({mode:"block"})` + `withFabricationGuard()` + `withVerification()`): no fabrication, but `max_iterations`, nothing written. Trace step 8, verbatim ‚ÄĒ `thought: "Let me check what files are available in the current directory:"` then `action: find({"query":"rates exchange rate","scope":"web"})`. **It tried to list the directory; the nearest tool was a web search.** Rails off ‚áí confident fabrication; rails on ‚áí no fabrication, no abstention, no answer. Correct behaviour reachable by NEITHER. **FOUR DEFECTS, ONE DEAD END:** (1) **no directory-listing tool existed** ‚ÄĒ recovery path structurally absent ‚áí added `list-directory` (file-root sandboxed; codepoint sort, not `localeCompare`, so a model's listing does not depend on host locale). (2) **`getRecoveryHint` was dead on the default path** ‚ÄĒ it maps ENOENT‚Üíadvice and fired ONLY on the legacy text-parse driver; native function calling (default for every capable model) got a bare errno. A `tool_result` is one of only THREE channels that reach the model's context. (3) **`file-read` retried ENOENT 3√ó with backoff** ‚ÄĒ measured **307ms/miss**, pinned by a timing test; and reported `File read failed: Error: ENOENT ...` (an `Error` interpolated into a template ‚áí double `Error:` prefix) with **no working root**, so a model-invented relative path was unresolvable by construction. Now retries only `EBUSY/EAGAIN/EMFILE/ENFILE` and names the root. (4) **`computeTrustReceipt` ignored `failed`** ‚ÄĒ rule was `ok > 0 && goalAchieved !== false`; a successful read of `orders.json` says nothing about the exchange rate. `failed` was computed ONE LINE ABOVE the verdict and read only into a display field. New rule: an **unresolved** tool failure (resolution is per `(tool, argument-fingerprint)`, so a retried transient failure still grounds) **AND** `goalAchieved !== true` ‚áí `partially-grounded`. **AFTER (same task, same models, rails off):** both ‚Üí `file-read` ‚Üí ENOENT+hint ‚Üí `list-directory` ‚Üí `config.json` ‚Üí **184.00**, `final_answer_tool`, `tool-grounded`. Without `list-directory` exposed the hint names no tool and the run **fails honestly** (`receipt: failed`) instead of fabricating. **This is a capability that was structurally ABSENT, not a statistical lift. No ablation was run; no accuracy/token claim is made.** **TWO REGRESSIONS ONLY THE LIVE RUNS CAUGHT:** (a) the first receipt rule keyed on `requiredTools` ("a required tool failed against a target it never read successfully") ‚ÄĒ but after `list-directory` shipped, haiku hit the **SAME ENOENT**, recovered via `config.json`, answered correctly, with an **identical failed-call signature**; the rule would have downgraded the best possible behaviour. It also read `this.config['requiredTools']`, which is **`undefined` on the non-streaming path** (`ReactiveAgent.config` holds 5 keys), so it was inert there regardless. **What separates fabrication from recovery is the ENDING:** `end_turn` (`goalAchieved: null`, documented "treat as maybe") vs `final_answer_tool` (`true`). (b) the hint named `list-directory` **unconditionally** ‚áí with a `{file-read, file-write}` toolbox haiku obeyed it, got `Tool call used unavailable name(s): list-directory`, and looped to `max_iterations` writing nothing ‚ÄĒ **strictly worse than the vague hint it replaced**. Keying off `toolService.listTools()` did NOT fix it: **that is the REGISTRY, not the model's toolbox** ‚ÄĒ built-ins are registered but withheld from the LLM schema unless opted in via `withTools({builtins})`. The exposed schema is the only honest source; **`ExecuteAndObserveCtx.schemas` is declared REQUIRED and `act.ts` never passed it** (the primitive read `undefined`) ‚ÄĒ wired both call sites (`act.ts` batch path + `tool-observe`). **OPEN, RANKED:** **P0 the model never sees its own reasoning** ‚ÄĒ `assembly/stages/project-results.ts:60` replays EVERY assistant turn as `{role:"assistant", content:"", toolCalls}`, and `AgentEvent` declares a `thought` kind (`event-log.ts:3`) with **ZERO writers** (`from-kernel-state.ts` never emits one). Tool results survive; derived conclusions, plans and self-corrections do not ‚ÄĒ while the persona says "think step by step". **Ablation-gated (changes every prompt); do NOT flip silently.** **P1 most "boosts" cannot reach the model** ‚ÄĒ only 3 channels carry information in: the goal, tool results, and a one-turn `Guidance:` tail appended to the SYSTEM prompt then cleared (`think.ts:372`, `guidance.ts:80`); pace, entropy, the ledger, requirement tracking and verifier verdicts all write to `state.steps` ‚áí they gate control flow and **cannot make the model smarter**. **P2 `find` is default-on with silent web egress** ‚ÄĒ `withTools({builtins:["file-read","file-write"]})` STILL exposes `find`, whose `scope:"auto"` falls back to **web search** at `riskLevel:"low"`; this is what haiku fabricated with. **Owner decision, not a silent fix.** **P3 the required-tool nudge FIGHTS the abstention rail** ‚ÄĒ rails-on trace steps 11/15: `‚ö†ÔłŹ Required tool quota not met: file-write. Call file-write NOW` (escalating) while the correct action was to decline; the gate tracks **tool names**, not required **entities** (`file-read` succeeded once on `orders.json` ‚áí the `file-read` requirement was satisfied though the required `rates.json` read failed). `fileReadTool` already declares `cardinality: "per-entity"`; **nothing consumes it.** **P4 inert census** ‚ÄĒ 5 ledger kinds never minted (`requirement`/`handoff` each have a live reader ALREADY WAITING: `assess.ts:207`, `standing-frame.ts:147/177`); 4 of 8 control proposers have zero production callers; `check-control-plane.sh` is green only because it **grandfathers the 4 forcing sites it exists to eliminate** (its own comment says the list "must SHRINK, never grow" ‚ÄĒ it never has); `guard.horizonProfile` is the **ONLY** plan field with a behaviour reader ‚áí the mid-run DEEPEN/LEAN recompile is a **behavioural no-op**; `verifierTier` = 4 tiers / 1 implementation / 0 tier-dispatch; compaction triggers at `window * 4` chars ‚Čą the FULL context window (`compact-history.ts:20`) so it effectively never fires, and failed tool output is `preserveOnCompaction: true` ‚áí **pinned for the whole run**. **MEMORY CORRECTIONS (prior claims were WRONG):** `result.verified` **does not exist** as a result field; the H5 honest-label fields (`harnessAuthoredOutput`, `budgetTerminalPartial`) **now DO have** a behaviour reader (`completion-status.ts:41‚Üí56`), wired into `reactive.ts` and `direct.ts` only, while `verificationWarning` remains write-only. `deriveReceiptDeliverables` on the non-stream path reads `this.config['requiredTools']`/`['taskContract']` ‚ÄĒ **both always `undefined`** ‚áí pre-existing, unfixed. **TOOLS VERDICT:** descriptions are genuinely model-facing and good; the rust is that `file-write`'s description literally pleads *"do NOT use 'file', 'filename', or 'filepath'"* (a scar where argument-alias coercion belongs), two terminators ship (`task-complete` + `final-answer`), three memory tools overlap (`recall`/`checkpoint`/`scratchpad`), and `rag-search`/`scratchpad` are marked superseded yet still exported. **PROCESS SCARS:** `git stash push -- <path>` created NO stash (no changes at that path) and the follow-up `git stash pop` restored a **pre-existing 06-28 user stash** into the tree with conflicts (recovered ‚ÄĒ pop-with-conflict does not drop the stash; **check `git stash list` before popping**); `git checkout -- <file>` to restore after a mutation test **reverts to HEAD and wipes uncommitted work** (use `cp` backups); Python `open(p,"w").write(s)` round-trips introduced NUL bytes so git saw the source as **binary** (prefer `sed -i` / Edit). Every fix mutation-verified: dropping the verdict rule ‚áí 6 red; dropping only its `goalAchieved` conjunct ‚áí red on the RECOVERY case; dropping the target fingerprint ‚áí 3 red; restoring the ENOENT backoff ‚áí red on the 307ms timing pin; naming the tool unconditionally ‚áí reproduces the `max_iterations` bug. core 177 / tools 957 / runtime 1242 / reasoning 2291 / benchmarks 290 pass, 0 fail; full `turbo run build` green. Debrief: `wiki/Research/Debriefs/2026-07-09-harness-capability-audit-debrief.md`.
- 2026-07-09 **THE CONTROL-PLANE SEAMS WERE INERT ‚ÄĒ in-loop abstain was unreachable** (`241e7efe`, `e7078395`). `deriveInLoopForcedAbstention` summed `synthesisRetryCount + groundingBlockRetry` vs `FORCE_UNGROUNDED_THRESHOLD = 2`, but mid-loop `synthesisRetryCount` is **capped at 1** (`arbitrator.ts` `SYNTHESIS_RETRY_MAX`) and `groundingBlockRetry` increments **only POST-loop** ‚áí max sum **1 < 2**; the other branch needs `iterationsRemaining<=0`, true mid-loop only at `iteration===0` (before F3 needs ‚Č•2 failures, before stall needs `iteration>=2`). ‚áí **`inLoopAbstentionProposal` returned null at EVERY seam**: F3 (`a102bcc9`), stall (`69c4ef9e`), AND the original strategy-switch P5 fix. All inert in production. **My own seam tests passed because they set `meta.synthesisRetryCount = 2` ‚ÄĒ impossible in production.** Unit-testing `f()` with an input `f` can never receive; committed twice in one day. - 2026-07-09 **CONTROL-PLANE SEAM SWEEP ‚ÄĒ 2 of 6 emitters wired, 4 verified NO-DELTA** (`a102bcc9`, `69c4ef9e`). **The reusable seam pattern:** at any seam that FORCES a control action, build `[<seam emitter>, inLoopAbstentionProposal(...)]`, call `resolveControlPlane`, `emitControlResolution`, and on `abstain` route through the single-owner `terminate()`. Gate behind `horizon !== undefined` so the default path is byte-identical; commit the seam's counter ONLY if the seam's action WINS. **(a) `a102bcc9` F3 seam** (`iterate-pass.ts:974`): forced its `redirect`(4) and `return "continue"`d; the in-loop abstain proposal was only built at the strategy-switch seam (needs loop detector). abstain(1) > redirect(4). A run with NO deliverable + exhausted ungrounded-synthesis retries was NUDGED instead of declining. Measured long-horizon: before iter 4 + 2 nudges; after iter 2 + 0 nudges. Default pinned byte-identical (4/2). **DO NOT WIRE the other 4 ‚ÄĒ verified no-delta, wiring = write-only:** `proposeFromGroundedTerminal` (`applyGroundedTerminalGate` already resolves redirect‚Üíabstain via single owner `evaluateTerminalGate` w/ bounded budget; only runs on `exit-success` so a veto pre-empts it); `proposeFromDispatcher` (**measured**: an ungrounded `dispatcher-early-stop` with fabricated output ALREADY abstains at iteration 1 in BOTH profiles ‚ÄĒ the "ships a clean success" hypothesis was REFUTED by execution); `proposeFromControllerVeto` (veto is priority 0, evaluator runs FIRST, nothing outranks); `proposeFromBudgetMonitor` (budget/error hard-stops are the SOLE proposal at their site by design, `control-plane.ts:140-143`). **CORRECTION ‚ÄĒ `emitters.ts`'s "wrong remedy" doc claim is FALSE:** `RecoverySteeringKind` is only `"stall" | "loop"` and the "stall" text already names the failing tool + asks for corrected args; **nothing reads `ControlRemedy`**. - 2026-07-09 **VERIFY PHASE WAS UNREACHABLE + CONTROL PRECEDENCE INVERSION** (`f466eb13`, `a102bcc9`). **(1) The `verify` phase could NEVER be entered.** The audit's "assess ignores `verdict.verified`" was a SYMPTOM. `assess()` keyed verify off `gate:"terminal"` verdicts, minted at only two sites (`arbitrator.ts:1335` exit-success, `:1367` exit-failure), both of which transition to `done`/`failed` and END the loop; `assess()` runs per-iteration INSIDE the loop (`iterate-pass.ts:468`) ‚áí the predicate was ALWAYS false and `PHASE_PROFILES.verify` was dead render code. The only test producing "verify" (`assess.test.ts:181`) hand-fed the ledger. **Root: `gate:"in-loop"` ‚ÄĒ the third declared verdict gate ‚ÄĒ had ZERO writers.** Fix mints it in `step-projection.ts` from observation steps the guards ALREADY write (`completion-guard` think.ts:1595, `abstention-legitimacy` think.ts:1284), keyed on `observationResult.toolName`; minting stays inside `kernel/ledger/` so `check-ledger-writes.sh` holds; the gate set is **CLOSED** (an open set pins every run to verify, since ordinary tool observations also project). `assess()` now reads the LATEST in-loop/terminal verdict ‚ÄĒ a REJECTED in-loop verdict ‚áí verify/repair, an ACCEPTED one ‚áí about to terminate. **That is what finally makes `.verified` load-bearing.** Pinned via real chokepoints (`transitionState`‚Üíledger‚Üí`assess`‚Üí`fromKernelState`/`project`‚Üí`request.systemPrompt`); mutation-verified (revert assess ‚áí 2 red; drop the mint ‚áí 6 red). **(2) F3 seam let `redirect` beat `abstain` by CODE ORDER.** `resolveControlPlane`'s total order is veto(0) > abstain(1) > terminate(2) > strategy-switch(3) > redirect(4) > steer(5), but the F3 seam (`iterate-pass.ts:974`) FORCED its redirect and `return "continue"`d, while the in-loop abstain proposal was built ONLY at the strategy-switch seam (needs the loop detector to trip). Same inversion as P5, second seam. `proposeFromErrorRecovery` existed to fix exactly this and had **zero production callers** (all refs in `emitters.test.ts` ‚ÄĒ unit-tested into looking done). Measured on real `runKernel`‚Üí`iteratePass`, long-horizon: **before** iteration 4/4 + 2 redirects + post-loop abstain; **after** iteration 1 + 0 redirects + in-loop abstain (3 wasted iterations). Redirect counter only commits if the redirect WINS. Gated behind long-horizon; default path pinned byte-identical to the measured baseline. **CORRECTION ‚ÄĒ do NOT act on `emitters.ts`'s "wrong remedy" doc claim: it is FALSE.** `RecoverySteeringKind` is only `"stall" | "loop"`, and the "stall" text already names the failing tool and asks for corrected arguments. Wiring the emitter for its `ControlRemedy` metadata would be **write-only ‚ÄĒ nothing reads `ControlRemedy`.** The defect was precedence, not text. **BOARD: 1 of 6 control emitters wired.** Remaining need per-seam analysis (a wiring that changes no behavior IS the trap): `proposeFromControllerVeto`, `proposeFromBudgetMonitor`, `proposeFromStallGuard`, `proposeFromGroundedTerminal`, `proposeFromDispatcher`. **4th form of the disease ‚ÄĒ *checked, but exempted*:** `check-control-plane.sh` is GREEN because it grandfathers the 4 files that still force control directly (incl. `runner.ts` ¬ß7.5); its own comment says the list "must SHRINK, never grow" ‚ÄĒ it hasn't. - 2026-07-09 **H5 HONESTY P0 FIXED + GRADED METRIC** (`3e87f9d5`, `1933f871`). **H5:** harness could return `result.success===true` beside `verified:false`. `runner.ts:1220` (`onlyHarnessAuthorshipFailed`) kept `status:"done"`; `reactive.ts` mapped done‚Üí"completed"; `reasoning-post-think.ts:85` derives `success = status==="completed"`. - 2026-07-09 **WIRING AUDIT ‚ÄĒ "BUILT, NEVER WIRED"** (HEAD `385bb686`; report `wiki/Research/Audit-Reports-2026-07-09/00-SYNTHESIS-wiring-audit.md`). **ONE DISEASE:** a mechanism built correctly, then never wired to anything that can fail ‚ÄĒ 3 forms: *computed-never-read*, *read-never-written*, *checked-never-run*. **STANDING RULE (owner):** a mechanism is DONE only when (1) a non-test consumer READS it and BEHAVIOR CHANGES (trace/receipt-only reads are still write-only ‚ÄĒ say so), (2) a test FAILS WHEN THE WIRING IS CUT (unit-testing `f()` ‚Č† pinning that `f()` is called), (3) if an invariant script guards it, something EXECUTES that script. **3 P0s FIXED:** (a) `a042e2f9` ‚ÄĒ `.withContract({tools:[{kind:"forbidden"}]})` was SILENTLY UNENFORCED (`task-contract.ts:33` promises "MUST NOT be visible to the LLM"; the constraint had ZERO readers, `tool-surface.ts` had no deny filter). Now `forbiddenTools(contract)` + Stage-0 filter over `universe`/`visible`/`callable`; deny beats required/allowed/META; mutation-verified. Executed proof: identical 4.0pp lift ‚Üí `default-on` at n=1, `opt-in` at n>1. `evaluateLiftGate` had ZERO production callers. Now: SE-of-difference bar, Agresti-smoothed spread ‚ąö(pŐÉ(1‚ąípŐÉ)) pŐÉ=(x+1)/(n+2) (strictly positive at every n), NEW **`underpowered`** verdict + `minRuns:3` + `runsNeeded`, `--gate <base>,<cand>`, and an UNCONDITIONAL power warning on every multi-variant session. (2) **`globalThis.fetch = mockAgentEndpoint(...)` in back-compat tests never restored** ‚Üí SSE "hel/lo" fixture answers every request 200. Fix: `packages/react/tests/happy-dom.ts` `withHappyDom()` helper (beforeAll register + afterAll unregister, guarded), wired into all 8 react test files; `afterEach` fetch restore in react+svelte `back-compat` tests; `generate-metrics.ts` now counts `.tsx` test files (was undercounting 908‚Üí900). **Debug lessons: bun runs test files SEQUENTIALLY single-process (proved via A/B setTimeout probe) ‚ÄĒ a non-restoring global mutation persists to later files; `--include=*.ts` grep MISSES `.tsx` (react) ‚ÄĒ the 2nd leaker hid there; isolate happy-dom register WITHOUT the fetch mock to prove which pollutant breaks victims.** Reinforces [[feedback_ci_parity_no_keys_no_ollama]]: turbo-green ‚Č† raw-`bun test`-green.

## ‚Ė∂ Agentic OS North Star v6.0 RATIFIED (2026-07-05) ‚ÄĒ CANONICAL forward direction

Spec: `wiki/Architecture/Specs/08-AGENTIC-OS-NORTH-STAR.md` (commit `28acc328`), successor to 05-DESIGN-NORTH-STAR ¬ß6 sequencing; 00-VISION pillars unchanged. Grounded in 10-subsystem parallel audit (2√ó5 explorers) + mid-2026 landscape research.

**Master finding: last-mile WIRING program, not building.** ~70-90%-built subsystems missing final wire (all file:line-cited in spec ¬ß1): A2A executor never bridged + server never started; `RunReport.skillFragment` never populated; UI protocol reserved tags (TrustEvent/StepEvent/UiTreeDelta/ObjectDelta) zero emitters; `checkOutput` zero runtime callers; kernel recall/learn = Noop layers; `authorize()` unconsumed; `ToolService.execute` enforces nothing; LLM I/O not captured on live path (replay = tool-surface only); trustVerdict bench-only; orchestration "durable" = in-memory Refs; 8/12 phase hooks dead; calibration = most under-surfaced shipped system.

**4 arcs:** (1) **Log+Process+Receipt** ‚ÄĒ one canonical event log w/ LLM I/O capture, RunHandle v2 (inspect/fork/grant/revoke, `rax ps/attach/fork`), `result.receipt` consolidating 5 disconnected trust systems; LAUNCH LINE here (bench receipts + Show-HN). (2) **Boundary+Gate** ‚ÄĒ enforce at execute(), wire authorize(), BYO lift-gate (unify packages/eval ‚ÜĒ benchmarks gate). (3) **Team** ‚ÄĒ A2A last mile, sub-agent events‚Üíparent bus, orchestration durability onto RunStore, MissionBrief/UpwardReport primitives, receipt chain. (4) **Flywheel** ‚ÄĒ skillFragment, learned aliases (act.ts:325 TODO), auto-calibration chain, harness packages w/ receipts, verifiable self-improvement LAST. **Dead-seam law: every dead seam goes live or gets deleted.** Non-goals carried: no new strategies, no falsified levers, no UI-binding race, lift gate on every default-on.

**Red-team amendments (`8c402be3`, user-ratified):** (1) **LAUNCH GATE = fixed 5-item demoable subset of Arc 1** (LLM I/O capture, inspect + rax ps/attach, fork v1, receipt v1, bench receipts published) ‚ÄĒ anti-slip vs the v0.11‚Üív0.13 deferral pattern; build-toward-visible-potential over launch-now. (2) **Honest-claims scoping:** fork = counterfactual restart NOT time-travel; zero-token CI = exact-replay only; receipt = graded evidence, Ed25519 signs provenance not correctness, false-verified rate published. (3) **Commons transparency contract:** telemetry default-on ONLY under first-run notice + opt-out + published schema + open aggregate data + never content/PII ‚ÄĒ else flips opt-in.

**Live-probe validation (`87a97daf`, 7 e2e Ollama probes ‚ÄĒ `wiki/Research/Harness-Reports/2026-07-05-north-star-live-probe-validation.md`):** north star CONFIRMED + sharpened. (1) Receipt gap visceral ‚ÄĒ result carries NO toolsUsed/trust fields. (2) pause/resume/stop WORK live; inspect/fork absent. (3) **Durable checkpoints kernel-path (`.withReasoning()`) ONLY ‚ÄĒ silent no-op on run()/inline** + unknown builder options swallowed ‚Üí NEW Arc 2 workstream "config truthfulness" (spec ¬ß5.2b). ## ‚úÖ Cortex Run Control ‚ÄĒ immediate abort (Phase C, MERGED to local main `67943256`, 2026-07-02)

Worktree `worktree-cortex-dynamic-sync` (same branch as Phase B capability-manifest). **Stop stays graceful (halts at next phase boundary); new Terminate is immediate ‚ÄĒ aborts the in-flight LLM call.** 6 commits `67948fba`‚Üí`4a772604`, TDD, 93 combined tests green. **Live-verified on Ollama: gemma4:12b generation terminated@800ms ‚Üí run() settled@805ms.**

- **C1** `packages/guardrails/src/kill-switch.ts` ‚ÄĒ `KillSwitchService` gains per-agent `AbortController` map + `signal(agentId)`; `terminate()` aborts it (`ensureController` so a terminate racing ahead of `signal()` still yields an aborted controller).
- **C2 ‚ÄĒ the plan's premise was WRONG, worth remembering.** Plan claimed "the LLM complete/stream signal option is already honored by providers" ‚ÄĒ FALSE: `LLMRequest` has no signal field and anthropic/openai ignore any signal. The real abort seam is **Effect fiber interruption**: Ollama's `Effect.tryPromise((signal)=>‚Ä¶)` forwards the fiber-interrupt signal to its fetch (`llm-provider/src/providers/local.ts:413`). Fix threads the killswitch `AbortSignal` into `runtime.runPromise(effect, { signal })` at the `run()` seam (`runtime/src/reactive-agent.ts:767`). **CRITICAL gotcha: acquire via `Effect.serviceOption(KillSwitchService)`, NOT bare `KillSwitchService.pipe(...)` ‚ÄĒ a missing service is an Effect DEFECT that `catchAll` does NOT catch, and this runs on EVERY run() ‚Üí the bare form broke 133 runtime tests (any run without `.withKillSwitch()`).** On a mid-flight abort it emits `AgentTerminated` (phase-boundary parity) + a clean terminal error.
- **C3** `apps/cortex/server/services/runner-service.ts` ‚ÄĒ `terminate(runId)` + shared **idempotent** `finalizeRun` (atomic claim from `activeRef` ‚Üí no double-dispose/double-unsubscribe when terminate races the run's own `.finally`); `ActiveEntry` now carries `unsubscribe`.
- **C4** `POST /api/runs/:runId/terminate` (mirrors stop). **C5** `run-store.terminate()` + confirm-gated Terminate button beside Stop in `RunDetail.svelte` (live + paused states).
- Rebuilt runtime+guardrails dist so the Node-consumer Cortex server picks up C2 (workspace `bun` export runs framework from src for probes/tests, but the built server reads dist). Pre-existing runtime fails NOT introduced: model-routing√ó2 (need keys), built-surface (needs dist). Remaining in the effort: generic field renderer + Phase A (model-routing UI) + Phase D (rerun).

## ‚ö†ÔłŹ File-root sandbox escape FOUND+FIXED (2026-07-02)

REAL production bug, found while investigating why RA scored near-bottom on file-output tasks in the public competitor bench (not a security audit). Tool-call healing pipeline (`packages/tools/src/healing/path-resolver.ts resolvePaths`) is a correct safety net ‚ÄĒ expands relative file-tool paths against a `workingDir` root and remaps hallucinated absolute paths back into it. But 3 call sites fed it `process.cwd()` instead of the tools package's own `getFileRoot()` (the AsyncLocalStorage-backed sandbox root `withFileRoot()` sets ‚ÄĒ the file-write/file-read handlers themselves already correctly used it): `reasoning/src/kernel/capabilities/act/act.ts:188` (react-kernel, ALL reasoning strategies route single/parallel-batch calls through here), `reasoning/src/strategies/plan-execute/step-executor.ts:203`, `reasoning/src/strategies/blueprint/worker.ts:240`. Net effect: any relative/hallucinated-absolute path a model passed to file-write got pre-resolved OUTSIDE the sandbox before the handler's own traversal guard ran ‚ÄĒ which then correctly rejected it with "Path traversal detected". **NOT benchmark-only: file-root sandboxing silently failed for ANY reasoning-strategy agent (react/plan-execute/blueprint ‚ÄĒ most real usage) with file-write tools inside a `withFileRoot()` scope.**

**Diagnosis method (reusable):** (1) ruled out timeout/infra contamination first via `status=error && tokensUsed=0` signature scan, infra-wide not RA-specific; (2) traced one failing cell's `benchmark-traces/<traceId>.jsonl` ‚ÄĒ `tool-call-start` count > `tool-call-end`, `guard-fired` event with the error text; (3) minimal `withFileRoot()`+`agent.run()` repro ‚ÄĒ worked WITHOUT `.withReasoning()`, broke WITH it; (4) instrumented `getFileRoot()` directly at point of failure ‚ÄĒ ALWAYS correct (ruled out ALS/Effect-fiber propagation loss, first hypothesis); (5) the arg reaching the handler was already wrong ‚ÄĒ traced upstream to healing pipeline's `workingDir` param, found `process.cwd()` hardcoded at all 3 sites. **LESSON: getFileRoot() being correct everywhere it's directly called doesn't mean the sandbox holds ‚ÄĒ a pre-processing stage (arg healing) can silently reintroduce the unsandboxed value if it has its own copy of "what's the working dir" logic instead of calling the shared accessor.**

Fixed `78bd31ac` ‚ÄĒ all 3 sites now pass `getFileRoot()`. Verified: hand repro (bug‚Üífix confirmed, file lands in correct sandbox), regression test `reasoning/tests/kernel/act/file-root-healing.test.ts` (3 cases), full `tools` (889/0) + `reasoning` (1866/0) suites green, tsc clean both. **Landed AFTER v0.13.0 shipped same day ‚ÄĒ not in the released tarball. v0.13.1 patch not yet cut, needs user confirm** (real security-adjacent gap, worth considering).

## ‚Ė∂ Public Competitor Bench ‚ÄĒ v0.13 Receipts deliverable (2026-07-07: qwen3:14b re-run DONE, publication posture pending user review)

**QWEN3:14B RE-RUN (2026-07-07, post-Arc-1 main, report `wiki/Research/Harness-Reports/2026-07-07-public-competitor-bench-qwen3-14b-rerun.md`):** RA wins ALL 3 execution tasks (resilience +100, multi-file +33, memory +33); loses both research tasks (fabrication under forced grounding, probe-traced: noisy web-search ‚Üí qwen invents EdgeVec/LiveBlocks; judge correctly 0s). Aggregate 35% = LOWER BOUND (10/45 RA cells timed out/abandoned; zombie fibers contend GPU). Integrity: error-cell judge short-circuit FIXED (`scoreErrorCell`); zombie-fiber abort OPEN. Judge recipe: `JUDGE_LAYER=live JUDGE_PROVIDER=openai JUDGE_MODEL=gpt-4o-mini` ‚ÄĒ WITHOUT JUDGE_LAYER a silent STUB scores 0.95 everything. ALWAYS pass `--output`. Posture: cogito 44% headline (clean run), qwen per-task pattern w/ timeout caveat, fabrication finding published as open problem.

**FIXES VERIFIED WITH REAL LIFT** (cogito:8b re-run, clean, 0 timeouts/0 judge errors): ra-full accuracy 29%(orig baseline)‚Üí16%(F1/F3 shipped but bench never wired KernelInput.requiredTools, so F1 was inert)‚Üí**44%** after ALSO fixing the bench wiring (`d26e8695`: fixture-bearing tasks call `.withRequiredTools({tools: builtins})` ‚ÄĒ the default adaptive-classifier path silently resolves empty for weak local models, a separate pre-existing gap, not F1's own bug). 44% now decisively best of 6 variants (bare 33%, manual-react 33%, langchain 20%, vercel 20%, mastra 27%). memory-under-compaction 0%‚Üí**67%** (the exact F2-targeted task). Honest trade-off worth publishing as-is: reliability dropped 59%‚Üí43% (`claimed-success (unverified)` roughly doubled 5‚Üí10 as `dishonest-success-suspected` dropped 7‚Üí5) ‚ÄĒ model now genuinely attempts+often-succeeds at tools but claims aren't always independently verified. **Zero literal `terminatedBy:"abstained"` fired** ‚ÄĒ the win came from required-tools enforcement forcing real engagement + F2 arg-healing, not F1's 2nd-ungrounded-attempt abstention path directly (F1 itself is correct/unit-tested; this task set just doesn't trigger its specific threshold). **NEXT: same fixed harness against qwen3:14b, re-verify.**

**qwen3:14b FINAL landed** (6/90 timeouts spread across variants incl bare-llm √ó3 ‚ÄĒ qwen thinking-spirals at 420s; 0 judge errors): ra-full accuracy 49% ‚ÄĒ beats bare (27%)/langchain (44%)/vercel (40%)/mastra (48%) but **manual-react wins at 77%**. RA Full wins the 3 hard execution tasks (memory-compaction +100%, resilience +67%, multi-file-debug +33%), regresses the 2 research tasks (-33%, -53%). **Cross-model story: harness wins where execution is hard, hurts where the model could just answer ‚ÄĒ diagnosed defect, not noise.**

**ROOT CAUSE DIAGNOSED** (`wiki/Research/Harness-Reports/2026-07-02-cogito8b-competitor-bench-root-cause.md`): runtime never enforces what diagnosis detects. Early ungrounded end_turn reaches NO enforcement: recovery steering = stall/loop-gated (never fires at iter 1-2); forced abstention's "‚Č•2 ungrounded synthesis" unreachable (first synthesis terminates run); verifier `action-success` = final-answer call's own flag only; `output-not-continuation-intent` = last-line-only (multi-paragraph plan-narrations pass ‚ÄĒ rw-7 shipped "First, let's check using brief()..." as a PASSING final answer, 8/8 checks). Even rw-1's acc=1 "wins" hallucinated every tool name (parametric luck) ‚Üí reliability 59% = same defect. Honesty across ra-full: 0/15 verified successes. Token tax ~10√ó (7.3k vs 708 bare). **Fixes dispatched 2026-07-02: F1 grounded-terminal invariant + F3 repeated-identical-failure escalation (kernel-warden), F2 arg-shape unwrap healing (tools-warden).** After verify: re-run smoke + both models ‚Üí publish honest before/after.

**cogito:8b FINAL clean dataset landed** (0/90 timeouts, 0 judge errors, 0 inconclusive/partial): Task table (Bare LLM/RA Full/Lift) ‚ÄĒ research-synthesis 100%‚Üí67% (-33%, single-run noise on small sample), data-investigation 0%‚Üí13% (+13%), multi-file-debug 0%‚Üí0%, memory-under-compaction 0%‚Üí0%, resilience-under-tool-failure 0%‚Üí67% (+67%). Dimension means: accuracy bare-llm 20% vs ra-full 29% (best of all 6 variants; competitors 9-27%); reliability lowest for ra-full (59% vs 74-100% others) ‚ÄĒ real nuance worth noting in the writeup, not obviously a bug. Raw: `benchmark-traces/`, report JSON in scratchpad `public-competitor-cogito-8b-final.json`.



RA vs LangGraph.js/Vercel AI SDK/Mastra on local models via Ollama (plan 2.2). Infra `f34d249f`: `benchmarks/src/competitors/ai-sdk-model.ts` (shared AI-SDK model builder; Ollama via OpenAI-compat `/v1`, none of the pinned competitor SDKs have a native Ollama adapter), langchain/mastra/vercel runners extended, `sessions/public-competitor-bench.ts` (qwen3:14b + cogito:8b, one model per session for strict GPU serialization, rw-1/2/7/8/9, 3 runs, 6 variants: bare-llm/manual-react/langchain-react/vercel-ai-sdk/mastra-agent/ra-full).

**3 real bugs found+fixed before any data trustworthy ‚ÄĒ do not skip this discipline on future bench sessions:** (1) ablation-table display bug ‚ÄĒ "RA Full" column pulled `bestVariantId` (often a competitor with 6 variants) while Lift was computed as `ra-full-bare-llm`, desyncing columns (75%‚Üí95% showed as "-75%"); (2) timeout too tight ‚ÄĒ 240s cap, 13/90 cells (14%) hit hard 0-token timeouts, infra-wide not RA-specific, legit durations already hit 228-231s; bumped to 420s + added `public-competitor-smoke` session (1 task/1 run/6 variants, run before any full session) ‚ÄĒ both `5dce62fd`; (3) [[file-root sandbox escape above]] ‚ÄĒ the big one, fixed `78bd31ac`.

**All bench runs so far are CONTAMINATED and discarded: qwen3:14b√ó2 attempts (OOM-killed, then display+timeout-bugged), cogito:8b√ó2 full runs (one file-root-sandbox-contaminated pre-`78bd31ac`, one judge-credit-exhausted post-fix ‚ÄĒ see below).** NEXT: re-run smoke ‚Üí full cogito:8b ‚Üí full qwen3:14b, all post-`78bd31ac` AND post-judge-switch, before publishing anything.

**4th anomaly ‚ÄĒ judge ran out of Anthropic credits, looked like more OOM fallout.** After a real system OOM killed one cogito run, a retry produced an ALL-DIMENSIONS-ZERO report (only `reliability` nonzero). Evidence field said `"Judge error: Judge RPC failed: 500 <!doctype html>..."` ‚ÄĒ the judge-server's Anthropic account hit `400 Your credit balance is too low`, every judge call threw, Bun served its HTML error page, bench recorded `score=0` everywhere the judge was consulted. **Symptom signature: every dimension exactly 0% across every variant except one (reliability, which doesn't route through the judge) ‚Üí judge-pipeline failure, not a real result ‚ÄĒ check `evidence` for "Judge error"/HTML first.** Fixed by restarting judge-server on `JUDGE_PROVIDER=openai JUDGE_MODEL=gpt-4o-mini` (already-provisioned key, satisfies Rule 4 separation from local Ollama SUT). **Verify judge health with a REAL POST to `/judge`, not just `/version`** ‚ÄĒ `/version` stays up even when the LLM backend is out of credits. Judge-server started detached (`setsid nohup ... & disown`).

**Diagnosis discipline that worked:** never accept a headline number without checking (a) timeout/error distribution per variant, (b) whether a losing dimension's judge `evidence` field explains a real gap vs an artifact, (c) trace files for the actual tool-call sequence when a result looks surprising. 3 of 4 anomalies this session were bugs/infra, not findings.

- **Env:** Cortex = Node-runtime consumer (own tsconfig, no `src` path map) ‚Üí server/UI tests need framework **built to dist** (`bunx turbo run build --filter='./packages/*'`) first.

## ‚Ė∂ Cost-Aware Model Routing SHIPPED to main (2026-06-30, for 0.13.0)

`.withModelRouting(options?)` ‚ÄĒ OPT-IN (off by default), routes each run to the cheapest CAPABLE model of the configured provider by task complexity, on BOTH inline + reasoning paths. Provider-agnostic (cost ladder haiku/sonnet/opus mapped per-provider via PROVIDER_CONFIGS; `isRoutableProvider`=Object.hasOwn(PROVIDER_CONFIGS,p) ‚ÄĒ DYNAMIC, no hardcoded list), capability-gated (never below a model whose ctx-window fits), advisory (degrades to configured model on error). Completed the built-but-dead router (was Anthropic-only, no public API, DEAD on reasoning path: reasoning-think.ts:256 fed defaultModel; kernel think.ts:611 stream omitted `model`). Full brainstorm‚Üíspec‚Üíplan‚ÜíSDD (5 tasks + opus whole-branch review + fix wave). Merged 91fb3c86; docs 32b7feca (cost-tracking.md + builder-api.md + whats-new). **DURABLE LESSONS: (1) tsup/`bun run build` PASSES despite real `tsc --noEmit` errors ‚Üí run tsc separately as the type gate; (2) 2 implementer green-suite claims masked real defects (streaming regression falsely called "pre-existing"; masked tsc errors) ‚ÄĒ ALWAYS independently re-verify subagent "all green"; (3) streaming regression root cause: `runGuardedPhase` BYPASSES phase.skip ‚Üí cost-route ran for streaming, threw on provider "test" ‚Üí Effect DEFECT killed stream fiber (fix: in-run guard + Effect.try; latent smell: skip-bypass also hits guardrail/strategySelect); (4) reasoning path ignores .withLayers (ReasoningServiceLive captures LLMService at construction) ‚ÄĒ capture model via EventBus LLMExchangeEmitted; (5) .withTestScenario forces provider=test ‚Üí routing degrades.** Also fixed a pre-existing main tsc error (verificationStep loop leftover from 157453e9). Detail: `~/.claude/.../memory/project_cost_aware_routing_2026_06_30.md`.

## ‚Ė∂ Test-Suite Health Audit + E2E Verification (2026-06-30)

**FINDING #1 RETRACTED ‚ÄĒ FALSE ALARM.** Earlier claim ".withFabricationGuard/.withStallPolicy absent from the built package" was WRONG: the probe ran from `/tmp` (outside the repo), so `import "reactive-agents"` resolved to bun's GLOBAL install cache = the stale PUBLISHED v0.12.0 tarball, not the workspace. From inside the repo both methods are present + callable; they're simply UNRELEASED (runtime src 0.10.6; committed June 27). **Durable rule: probe/verify ONLY from inside the repo ‚ÄĒ a /tmp probe silently tests the last published package.**

**Session pivot (user directive):** dedicate session to E2E-verifying existing features + auditing TEST-SUITE HEALTH (green-but-lying tests), fix issues, patch the regression nets that missed them. Baseline `bun test`: 6634 pass / 4 fail / 23 skip / 820 files / 96s. Method: 4 parallel audit agents (assertion-free ¬∑ over-mock ¬∑ error-path ¬∑ skipped/drift) + in-repo live verification. **ūüźõ REAL HIDDEN BUG FOUND+FIXED:** `withMinIterations(N)` under-enforced ‚ÄĒ `minIterations:3` made only 2 LLM calls; both enforcement sites (`inline-harness-hooks.ts:91` direct-LLM + `reasoning-harness-hooks.ts:159` reasoning) were a lone `if` (one retry) not a loop to N ‚Üí run finalizing at iter 1 got 1 extra pass regardless of N, breaking the "block early exit before N iterations" contract. ## ‚Ė∂ Agentic Landscape 2025‚Äď2026 vs RA ‚ÄĒ Competitive Gap Analysis (2026-06-29)

6-stream deep research (reasoning, memory/context, frameworks, tool-use, reliability/eval/governance) + full RA v0.12.0 inventory. Report: `wiki/Research/2026-06-29-agentic-landscape-vs-reactive-agents.md`. **Industry thesis VALIDATES RA bets:** (1) "the harness IS the product" (same model+diff harness swings scores 10‚Äď34pp; community demands harness disclosure); (2) reasoning moved INTO model ‚Üí orchestration value moved to a THIN DURABLE harness (ToT/GoT/LATS = prod dead-ends, native reasoning absorbed them); (3) Bitter Lesson hits orchestration LOGIC not the LAYER (substrate+ops+verification is durable; build structure removable); (4) reliability+cost = battleground (88% pilots never ship); (5) verify with EXECUTION not opinion (intrinsic self-correct neutral-to-harmful w/o external signal); (6) security is action-layer (lethal trifecta, OWASP Agentic 2026). **RA SCORECARD ‚ÄĒ AHEAD:** deterministic-oracle eval + pass^k, structured-output at emission-boundary-only (Alignment-Tax fix), no-LATS/GoT + no-LLM-reverify (M3), blueprint/ReWOO, tier-aware + tool-sanitize + healing + relevantTools, 4-layer cognitive memory (rare LangMem club), durable crash-resume + HITL. **BEHIND/WHITE-SPACE:** KV-cache prefix stability + tool-masking (RA compaction/lazy-prune CHURNS prefix + dangles tool refs = fights 10√ó cost lever), long-horizon deep-agent harness (recitation-to-recency + file-offload + per-feature checkpoint + cross-session recovery + per-step decomp/verify), agentic security (tool-descriptor trust/MCP OAuth2.1/capability attenuation), abstention as first-class action, memory formation discipline (hot-path vs background, verify-then-commit gate, relevance-gated retrieval, memory-evolution, Anthropic memory-tool /memories protocol, SKILL.md compat). **RANKED OPPORTUNITIES:** T1 ‚ÄĒ O1 cache/context efficiency (10√ó cost, pure win), O2 long-horizon deep-agent harness (top 2026 momentum, RA owns substrate), O3 deterministic-verify+abstention as TRUST BRAND. T2 ‚ÄĒ O4 cheap-first cascade routing + pre-call cost gate, O5 code-as-action first-class tiered action space + progressive tool disclosure, O6 retrieval-over-tools >100. T3 ‚ÄĒ O7 OTel-GenAI conventions, O8 memory formation discipline. T4 ‚ÄĒ O9 agentic security suite (biggest white-space, heaviest, later campaign). **RECOMMENDED: lead O1+O2, anchor O3** (all press RA advantages, not me-too). Detail: `~/.claude/.../memory/project_agentic_landscape_2026_06_29.md`. **Awaiting build direction.**

Systemic but LATENT for anthropic (never sets `thinking`) / openai (never sets `reasoning_effort`) ‚ÄĒ only Gemini (thinking-on default) breaks today. ## ‚Ė∂ Config Serialization Drift Closure + Anti-Drift Guard (2026-06-28)

Agent-as-data roundtrip (`AgentConfig`‚ÜĒbuilder) had drifted: 3 artifacts must agree ‚ÄĒ `AgentConfigSchema` (agent-config.ts), `serializeBuilder()` (builder/to-config.ts), `agentConfigToBuilder()` (agent-config.ts). Schema+deserializer grew; **serializer never updated** ‚Üí `toConfig()` silently dropped fields. Root cause: `builder.toConfig()` (builder.ts:2010) `serializeBuilder(this as unknown as BuilderStateForSerialization)` ‚ÄĒ cast severs typecheck so new schema field never forces serializer update. **DROPPED-FIELDS FIXED:** grounding, fabricationGuard, stallPolicy, taskContext, tools.focusedTools, reasoning.auditRationale, outputSchemaOptions (serialize-OUT only; schema obj not JSON). **DATA-PARITY ADDED (schema+ser+deser):** agentId, execution.minIterations, requiredTools, budget, circuitBreaker (incl `false`), rateLimiting, skillPersistence, durableRuns. ‚ö†ÔłŹ builder `BudgetLimits`={tokenLimit,costLimit,warningRatio} NOT cost-pkg {perRequest...}. `leanHarness` EXCLUDED (profile switch, force-disables memory ‚Üí can't coexist in one config). **DYNAMIC ANTI-DRIFT GUARD = `packages/runtime/tests/config-serialization-drift.test.ts`:** reads `AgentConfigSchema` AST at runtime, walks every leaf path ‚Üí (1) COVERAGE: MAXIMAL_CONFIG fixture must set every schema leaf (new field‚ÜíRED), (2) ROUNDTRIP: config‚Üíbuilder‚ÜítoConfig drops no leaf (missing ser/deser branch‚ÜíRED), (3) documented `NON_BUILDER_ROUNDTRIP` + exclusion-rationale prose. Future config can't drift silently. Verified: guard 3/3 (RED-first), agent-config 26/26, runtime 1037/0, build+DTS green. **SHIPPED local main (NOT pushed).** Detail: `wiki/Research/Debriefs/2026-06-28-config-serialization-drift-debrief.md`. Lesson: `as unknown as` at a serialization boundary is a drift magnet ‚ÄĒ AST-driven runtime guard + maximal fixture substitutes for the lost compile-time check.

## ‚Ė∂ Reasoning Strategy Portfolio + `blueprint` strategy (2026-06-28)

**RESEARCH-SHARPENED:** new strategy NAMED **`blueprint`** (was ReWOO). Web-validated: [Beyond-ReAct planner-centric DAG](https://arxiv.org/html/2511.10037v1) beats GPT-4 ReAct 59.8 vs 48.2 StableToolBench @2.29 steps; canonical 4th single-agent pattern. **Hard caveat: SLMs unreliable as standalone planners ‚Üí one-shot DAG fails on weak/local (our #1 req).** Fix = **PLAN‚ÜíVERIFY‚ÜíEXECUTE(0-LLM,parallel)‚ÜíSOLVE** (PACT). blueprint PLAN pours framework leverage into small-model planning: schema/grammar-ENFORCED gen (extractStructuredOutput, local jsonSchemaEnforcement = biggest lever) + calibration channel + numbered-step prompt + experience-tips inject + plan-VERIFY gate (deterministic valid-DAG/required-tools/refs + heal; degrade‚Üíreactive if invalid; local optional 1 critique-refine) + healing-in-Worker. NO fine-tuning variants (BYOK/local; design only). **‚úÖ blueprint SHIPPED 2026-06-28 (merged local main, NOT pushed; built via SDD): `strategies/blueprint/{worker,plan-verify}.ts` + `strategies/blueprint.ts`, registered `"blueprint"`+`"rewoo"`, 24 tests, reasoning 1797/0. PROOF-GATE (claude-haiku): rw-8 decomposable = blueprint 3.8k tok vs plan-execute 78.9k (~20√ó cheaper; both acc=0 = haiku model-bound on exact-output, parity); blueprint=1 LLM call(plan;solver short-circuit)+3 LLM-free file-writes. rw-9 observation-required = blueprint LOSES (acc0) vs plan-execute (acc1) ‚Üí domain boundary CONFIRMED. Ships OPT-IN. ‚ö†ÔłŹ raw-builder can't run plan-strategies (extractStructuredOutput fails for BOTH blueprint+plan-execute via builder; use bench runSession). **‚úÖ ADAPTIVE ROUTING SHIPPED 2026-06-28: adaptive heuristic+LLM-classifier route static-local-gen‚Üíblueprint, guards networkIO+observationDriven‚Üíplan-execute/reactive (rw-9 proof-gate evidence); local-tier keeps default-reactive (blueprint auto-routes mid/large/frontier only, local=opt-in); 8 routing tests, reasoning 1805/0 runtime 1021/0.** **‚úÖ BLUEPRINT VALIDATED both tiers 2026-06-28: rw-bp1 corpus task (create-3-files, deterministic node-check verify) ‚Üí frontier(haiku) acc=1/1734tok + local(qwen3:14b) acc=1/1721tok, both 1-LLM-call+3-LLM-free-writes. Tier-portability + small-model planning proven. ‚úÖ REACTIVE BATCH IMPROVED: parallel-batch tool calls now heal (shared healCall, was bypassing ‚Üí weak-model batched calls hard-failed); fixed healed-flag bug (call!==rawTc always-true ‚Üí actions.length>0, both paths) + added StallPolicy fields to KernelMeta type. reasoning 1806/0, runtime 1021/0.** Below = pre-build notes:

Pivot to strategy quality+efficiency. **Goal: portfolio of tier-portable strategies that each SHINE in a domain (not dead weight) + cross-cutting context/tool/memory/verify. All tiers local‚Üífrontier.** Scope: `wiki/Architecture/Design-Specs/2026-06-28-reasoning-strategy-portfolio.md`. Anti-goal: NO LATS/GoT/self-consistency (cost, no lift). **Build target: ReWOO** (plan tool-DAG once‚Üíexecute tools w/ 0 LLM‚Üísolve once = ~2 calls vs plan-execute ~9). Warden brainstorm: ReWOO GREEN (~80% infra exists = plan-execute minus reflect; Worker=`executeToolAndObserve` tool-observe.ts:159; #E DAG=`{{from_step:sN}}` plan.ts; ToolService.execute concurrency-safe, reuse `isParallelBatchSafeTool`). **Tier-portability driver = `calibration.parallelCallCapability` (reliable/partial/sequential-only) + `capability.toolCallDialect!=="native-fc"||source==="fallback"`‚Üítext-parse fallback.** ReWOO risks: loop-internal StallPolicy/required-tools bypassed by direct Worker (validate required-tools at PLAN time + self-budget); failed #E‚Üíempty args (fail-on-unresolved-ref); healing NOT in direct path (Worker must run runHealingPipeline). **‚úÖ SHIPPED pre-ReWOO (merged local main, NOT pushed): (1) Memory P0 ‚ÄĒ severed `experienceTips` loop (computed, never injected) ‚Üí `appendExperienceTips` in reasoning-think.ts, tier-capped (1 local/3 else), 5 tests. (2) tier-aware plan prompt (plan-execute.ts `modelTier:"mid"` hardcode ‚Üí resolveProfile). reasoning 1773/0, runtime 1018/0.** NEXT: parallel-tool Worker helper ‚Üí rewoo.ts ‚Üí proof-gate vs plan-execute rw-8/rw-9. Detail: [[project_strategy_portfolio_2026_06_28]].

## ‚Ė∂ Eval-driven harness sweep + honesty reframe (2026-06-26)

First weakness sweep USING the eval system as probe (cross-tier: qwen3:14b/cogito:14b/claude-haiku/gpt-4o-mini √ó bare-llm/ra-full). Report `wiki/Research/Harness-Reports/2026-06-26-cross-tier-weakness-sweep.md`. **‚ö†ÔłŹ CRITICAL: `analyzeRun` honesty label `claimed-success (unverified)` (analyze.ts:404-427) = "real work, no deliverable FILE" ‚ÄĒ NOT dishonesty; mislabels CORRECT text answers (rw-2@haiku acc=1.0 ‚Üí "unverified"). The "95% honesty crisis" was a misread ‚ÄĒ real signal ~50% claimed-but-wrong (overconfidence) + low absolute accuracy (gpt-4o-mini ra-full ‚Č§36%).** Always combine honesty label with judge accuracy. SHIPPED to main (local, NOT pushed): `ef0eb2be` verifier `output-not-continuation-intent` check (minority hardening, fired on 0 cells in re-bench ‚ÄĒ honest scope); `97c024f5` **`trustVerdict(honestyLabel, accuracyScore)`‚Üí`RunScore.trust`** (the REAL fix; offline-validated 4 verified-correct/5 claimed-but-wrong/1 honest-fail on real data, 16/16 + 126/0). Skill `harness-improvement-loop` updated to eval-system-as-primary-probe. **‚ö†ÔłŹ BENCH OPS: GPU = 16GB VRAM (4070 Ti Super) ‚ÄĒ constraint is VRAM budget NOT "no local". One big model resident = fast; >1 big spills to RAM ‚Üí 120s timeouts (14b Q4‚Čą9-10GB, 12b‚Čą7-8GB, small 3-4b‚Čą3-4GB; 14b SUT+gemma-12b judge‚Čą17GB>16=spill). Recipe: serialize SUTs (concurrency 1, ONE big at a time) + judge that co-resides (small 3-4b alongside 14b ‚Čą13GB) OR off-GPU (cloud/ollama-cloud, `OLLAMA_API_KEY` free-tier in .env). NEVER 2 big SUTs + big judge. Single 14b SUT alone = fast. ## ‚Ė∂ Canonical Evaluation & Improvement System (2026-06-24) ‚ÄĒ Phase 1 SHIPPED

Post-v0.12 direction: unify RA's **triple-fragmented** measurement infra into one canonical system. Infra is MATURE but split across 6 pkgs + a skill, three parallel stacks, **no shared spine**: `benchmarks` (matrix/ablation/9-variant ladder/5 competitor adapters, private) ¬∑ `eval` (5-dim judge, published, simpler) ¬∑ `trace` (`analyzeRun` honesty+failure-mode+blind-spot, **orphaned ‚ÄĒ no score links to its trace**) ¬∑ `judge-server` (FROZEN judge, SHA-pinned, Rule-4, production-ready) ¬∑ `diagnose`/`replay` ¬∑ `harness-improvement-loop` skill (manual). Fragmentation: 2 judges, 2 taxonomies (10 vs 5), 2 task models, 2 stores; industry alignment NOMINAL (named SWE-bench/GAIA but runs none).

**Plan:** canonical `Run` record (1 runId links score‚ÜĒtrace‚ÜĒdiagnosis); L0 corpus(+real industry adapters) ‚Üí L1 ONE frozen judge/ONE 10-dim ‚Üí L2 benchmarks matrix ‚Üí **L3 wire-the-why (attach analyzeRun to every Run ‚ÄĒ biggest dogfood win, mostly LINKAGE)** ‚Üí Lg `evaluateLiftGate` ‚Üí L4 ImprovementLedger(=B's substrate) ‚Üí L5 `rax eval` + honest public bench (‚Č•3 seeds, raw traces, stop-the-line >15%). Reframe: canonical JUDGE=frozen judge-server, ENGINE=benchmarks; candidate mutation = a `HarnessVariant` ‚Üí gate run = 2-variant ablation.

**SHIPPED ‚ÄĒ Phase 1 (Lg verdict), merged to LOCAL main `3e123eb7`, NOT pushed:** `packages/benchmarks/src/gate/` ‚ÄĒ `evaluateLiftGate(SessionReport, baselineVariantId, candidateVariantId, policy?) ‚Üí GateVerdict` (default-on|opt-in|reject) + `projectTierEvidence` + `formatGateReceipt`. Pure/sync/deterministic, 16 tests, build green. Rule: ‚Č•3pp ‚ąß ‚Č§15%tok ‚ąß ‚Č•2 tiers ‚ąß significant(per-cell variance=stddev) ‚ąß not-partial(inconclusive blocks default-on + excluded from aggregate). Tier=`modelVariantId`. **Unblocks B (verifiable self-improvement): gate IS B's validator.**

**SHIPPED ‚ÄĒ Phase 2 (contract-unify + dedup), merged to LOCAL main `e9d6216b`, NOT pushed:** 3 commits. (1) `@reactive-agents/core` now owns canonical `QualityDimension` (the 10 agentic dims) + `DimensionScore {dimension;score;evidence?}` + `CANONICAL_QUALITY_DIMENSIONS` (`core/src/contracts/score-contract.ts`, plain interfaces). (2) `benchmarks/types.ts` re-exports those from core (killed its duplicate decls ‚ÄĒ byte-identical, 98 tests green). (3) judge wire-contract deduped: `judge-server` type-exports its contract, `benchmarks/judge.ts` `import type`s it (deleted local mirror; type-only, no Effect bleed). **Decisions locked:** taxonomy = the 10 (safety‚Üíguardrail, relevance/completeness‚Üíaccuracy rubric, cost-efficiency‚Üíefficiency ‚ÄĒ all EXCLUDED + deferred); scope = contract-unify only, NO scoring-logic rewrite, **eval UNTOUCHED**. Plan: `wiki/Planning/Implementation-Plans/2026-06-25-eval-phase2-contract-unify.md`. 101 tests green, builds green.

**SHIPPED ‚ÄĒ Phase 3 (wire-the-why / L3), merged to LOCAL main `684358d9`, NOT pushed:** 6 commits, benchmarks-only (+ new `@reactive-agents/trace` dep). Attaches the "why" to every bench run: when `session.traceDir` set ‚Üí `.withTracing({dir})` ‚Üí `${traceDir}/<taskId>.jsonl` ‚Üí `loadTrace`‚Üí`analyzeRun`‚Üíslim `RunDiagnosis` {honestyLabel, honestyEvidence, failureModes[], blindSpots[]} on `RunScore.diagnosis` (+ `traceId`); flag-worthy runs print `‚ö† honesty=‚Ä¶ ¬∑ failure=‚Ä¶` under the row. **NO runtime change** ‚ÄĒ `AgentResult.taskId` already keys the trace (the user's "expose runId" fork was unnecessary). `diagnoseRun` best-effort (never throws); OPT-IN (no traceDir ‚Üí unchanged). **LIVE-verified end-to-end** (Anthropic run captured `diagnosis="dishonest-success-suspected"`). 107 tests green. Files: `benchmarks/src/diagnose.ts` (`projectDiagnosis`/`diagnoseRun`/`formatDiagnosisLine`), `types.ts` (`RunDiagnosis`+`RunScore.diagnosis?`), `runner.ts`. Real trace field is `blindSpots:{metric,reason}` (not `why`). Plan: `wiki/Planning/Implementation-Plans/2026-06-25-eval-phase3-wire-the-why.md`.

**SHIPPED ‚ÄĒ Phase 4 (gate CLI + CI), merged to LOCAL main `9104b7d0`, NOT pushed:** 3 commits + 2 fixes. `rax eval gate --report <SessionReport.json> --baseline <id> --candidate <id> [--metric/--min-lift/--max-tok/--min-tiers]` ‚ÄĒ reads a report (written by `rax bench --output`), applies pure `evaluateLiftGate`‚Üí`formatGateReceipt`, exits via pure `decideExitCode` (reject‚Üí1, no-comparable-tiers‚Üí2, default-on/opt-in‚Üí0). Report-mode = NO live models in the command. benchmarks DYNAMIC-imported (private pkg, matches bench.ts; only `import type` at module scope ‚ÄĒ NO static dep). `runEval` now `run|gate` dispatcher. Registered `frontier-spot-check` session (bare-llm vs ra-full, 4 frontier models) in bench CLI + `.github/workflows/regression-gate.yml` (workflow_dispatch: build‚Üíbench --output‚Üíeval gate‚Üífail-on-reject, secrets incl GOOGLE_API_KEY for the gemini model). Fixes: Gemini key in CI env, NaN-guard numeric flags. 111 tests green. Files: `apps/cli/src/commands/eval-gate.ts`. Plan: `wiki/Planning/Implementation-Plans/2026-06-25-eval-phase4-gate-cli.md`. **ImprovementLedger (L4) deferred.**

**SHIPPED ‚ÄĒ Phase 4b (ImprovementLedger / L4), merged to LOCAL main `27dba6ba`, NOT pushed:** 3 commits + 2 fixes. Code-owned gate-centric ledger in `@reactive-agents/benchmarks/src/ledger.ts`: records dogfood chain weakness‚Üíhypothesis‚ÜígateVerdict‚Üíregression-baseline. Deferred: cross-run baseline CHECK, B (autonomous loop reads ledger), skill back-link.

**KEY GROUNDED FINDINGS (for future phases):** the two judges already share ONE engine ‚ÄĒ `judge-server` *depends on* `eval`, wrapping eval's `JudgeLLMService` in an HTTP server (SHA-pinned/Rule-4); benchmarks calls it over HTTP. Dep graph: `core(pub)‚Üźeval(pub)‚Üźjudge-server(priv)‚Üźbenchmarks(priv,HTTP)`. benchmarks can't import eval (published‚Üíprivate) ‚ÄĒ hence contract lives in core. eval's in-process judge is NOT frozen (no SHA); judge-server adds the frozen wrapper. **Deferred:** eval taxonomy migration (fold rel/comp, safety‚Üíguardrail), eval reproducibility parity, P3 wire-the-why (attach `analyzeRun` to every Run ‚ÄĒ biggest dogfood win, mostly LINKAGE), P4 `rax eval gate` CLI/CI + facade, P5 industry adapters + publish (‚Üí v0.13 "Receipts"). Specs: `wiki/Architecture/Design-Specs/2026-06-24-canonical-evaluation-system.md` (umbrella) + `2026-06-24-eval-lift-gate-harness.md` + `wiki/Decisions/2026-06-24-high-leverage-roadmap-ranking.md`.

## ‚Ė∂ PERF: DEBRIEF OFF CRITICAL PATH ‚ÄĒ biggest harness latency lever, FIXED + MERGED to main (`787bd50d`, 2026-06-13)
Efficiency scan found the #1 waste: the post-answer debrief LLM call BLOCKED `run()`. **Measured (sonnet, memory ON): 4683ms of a 9847ms run = 48%**, AFTER the answer was produced (~6s local, GH #143). `execution-engine.ts:1059` "never blocks the result" was FALSE. **Fix (user Option C):** split `debrief-synthesis.ts` ‚Üí `prepareDebrief` (cheap fallback, inline) + `finalizeDebriefBackground` (LLM+persist, `Effect.forkDaemon`'d). `result.debrief`=instant fallback; new `result.debriefRich()` awaits the forked rich version lazily; `_debriefFiber` attached via Object.defineProperty; `_pendingDebriefs` Set joined by `dispose()` (forkDaemon interrupted by ManagedRuntime.dispose ‚Üí would drop persist). `result.metadata.tokensUsed` now = answer cost (debrief tokens background). **Re-measured: run() 9847‚Üí5297ms (~46% faster).** debrief-fork 3/3, trivial-gate 8/8, runtime 937/1 (1=pre-existing ceiling 68>66, +0 my casts), build 38/38. **Falsified levers stay dead** (cache-churn/extractObs-44%/local-step-economy/cogito-stall/escalation-lift). **MERGED 2026-06-13** (`787bd50d` ff; branch deleted; docs debrief-chat.md+builder-api.md updated, comment now truthful). **Finalize-tail scan VERDICT (2026-06-13): critical path now efficient ‚ÄĒ no large structural lever remains.** #2 runLocalLearning ‚ĚĆ FALSIFIED-CHEAP (`onRunCompleted` = pure local compute + WAL SQLite, NO LLM/network; "2.7s flush" was 100% debrief). Verified efficient 4 ways: tail=1 forked LLM call; batch tools already parallel (`act.ts:519` Effect.all concurrency); recall once-at-bootstrap not per-iter (Noop seam default); local-learning cheap. Remaining #3 qwen3 decode / #4 numCtx = LOCAL-tier model-specific tuning ONLY, bounded payoff, NOT structural. **Entropy double-embed lever FALSIFIED by ollama probe (2026-06-13): `llm=false` on every score call (LLMService not wired into EntropySensorService layer) ‚Üí semantic embed NEVER fires ‚Üí zero per-iter network cost; double-scoring real but cheap deterministic. PERF HUNT CONCLUDED ‚ÄĒ no major lever left.** New arch/honesty debt surfaced (NOT perf): semantic-entropy dead-by-default (`semanticEntropy:true` but inert) + redundant double-scoring. Tech-debt branch `fix/tech-debt-sweep-2026-06-13` (NOT merged): #1 as-unknown-as-ceiling 68‚Üí66 green (`ec56de71`, stale channel-service AgentEvent casts removed); #2 semantic-entropy sensor flipped default-OFF (`1f8c08d2`) ‚ÄĒ probe proved it non-functional via 3 bugs (llm-unwired + priorThought-never-populated + taskEmbedding-null/only-taskAlignment-surfaced); config was lying (`semanticEntropy:true` but inert). Verification-layer `enableSemanticEntropy` is SEPARATE, untouched. Re-enable needs all 3 fixed + ablation. Detail: [[project_debrief_off_critical_path_2026_06_12]].

## ‚úÖ OPT-IN EVIDENCE-GROUNDING ‚ÄĒ MERGED to main (`d40270ed`, 2026-06-11)
Numeric evidence-grounding now OPT-IN (`.withGrounding({mode:"block"|"warn"})`, default OFF). Killed the false `failed at evidence-grounded` verifier warnings on correctly-formatted `$` figures (old always-on byte-substring match vs COMPRESSED tool obs). When on: tolerant numeric VALUE match (`validateNumericGrounding`, parses `$`/commas/`k|M|B`) against FULL tool data (`buildEvidenceCorpusFromSteps(steps, scratchpad)` resolves `storedKey`‚Üíscratchpad). `block`=bounded corrective re-synthesis‚Üídegrade-to-warn (pure-capped `decideGroundingBlockOutcome`, dedicated `meta.groundingBlockRetry`, `hasNonGroundingBlock` guard so it NEVER rescues parrot/escalate; NOT M3 re-verify loop); `warn`=advisory softFail (untouched). **Scaffold-leak split out** ‚Üí standalone always-on `reject` guard (`scaffold-leak.ts` `detectScaffoldLeak`: `[STORED:]`/`_tool_result_N` echoed as answer). Prose claim-grounding REMOVED (64-73% false-reject). reasoning 1651/0, reviewer-clean. Detail [[project_opt_in_grounding_2026_06_11]].

## ūüĒī ORIGINAL FM-I REPORT (HIGH, GH #195, 2026-06-11) ‚ÄĒ see status above
Found by running scratch.ts LIVE (ollama gemma4:e4b, reflexion, `.on('observation.tool-result')` fired ZERO times despite tools running). Heavy/composite strategies hand-build `KernelInput` literal per call site, silently DROP cross-cutting fields `{harnessPipeline,budgetLimits,calibration,auditRationale,verifier}`. Code-verified drop matrix: reflexion `reflexion.ts:149,451`=0/5; plan-execute tool path `step-executor.ts:344`=0/5 (synthesis `plan-execute.ts:952` has only harnessPipeline); ToT `tree-of-thought.ts:189,647`=0/5 (`:599`=RI not kernel); adaptive drops before delegating; code-action bypasses kernel. Runtime supplies it (`runtime.ts:348`). **Consequences:** compose dead + killswitches don't fire mid-step (cost hole) + calibration off degrades LOCAL models (headline differentiator). **2nd occurrence of this class** (1st=MCP relevantTools drop) ‚Üí structural fix justified, validates strategy-consolidation. **Fix:** Phase 0 thread 5 fields + per-strategy `.on()`-fires test (ship first); Phase 1 mandatory `buildKernelInput()`; Phase 2 lint raw literals. v0.12 "Honest" item. ## ‚Ė∂‚Ė∂ CORTEX PARAMETERIZED RUNS ‚ÄĒ PHASE 1 SHIPPED (2026-06-08, branch `feat/cortex-parameterized-runs`)
Track B of the Cortex overhaul. Agent templates with `{{variable}}` placeholders filled at launch. **`apps/cortex` only ‚ÄĒ zero framework edits** (design forbids `packages/**`). 12-task plan executed via subagent-driven dev (impl + 2-stage review each). Spec `wiki/Architecture/Design-Specs/2026-06-06-cortex-parameterized-runs-design.md`; plan `wiki/Planning/Implementation-Plans/2026-06-06-cortex-parameterized-runs.md`.
- **One resolver, server-authoritative.** `server/services/resolve-template.ts` `resolveTemplate(input, variables, values)` deep-walks string leaves, substitutes `/\{\{\s*([\w.]+)\s*\}\}/g`; unknown/required-no-value tokens ‚Üí `unresolved[]` (left literal, never silently blanked). Client NEVER re-implements it ‚ÄĒ live preview delegates via `POST /api/template/resolve` (`{payload,variables,values}`‚Üí`{resolved,unresolved}`). Client `ui/src/lib/template/scan-template-vars.ts` is **authoring-only** (finds tokens, does not resolve).
- **`secret.` namespace RESERVED, not implemented** ‚ÄĒ `{{secret.X}}` always ‚Üí `unresolved` (extension seam for a future secret-store spec; smoke-confirmed).
- **Three launch paths wired:** (1) interactive Lab Run ‚Üí `ParamFillModal` (schema-driven fill + debounced live preview) when `builderConfig.variables.length>0`, else launch as before; (2) `POST /api/runs` threads `variables`+`variableValues`, **400 on unresolved** (FiberFailure.message===CortexError.message, string-match `includes` ‚ÄĒ instanceof does NOT survive `Effect.runPromise` boundary); (3) cron/gateway resolves from variable **defaults** (`gateway-process-manager.ts`, fails the scheduled run + records `error_message` via canonical `upsertRun`+`updateRunStats` if a required var has no default).
- **Authoring:** Variables editor section in `AgentConfigPanel.svelte` (auto-seed from `{{...}}` via Rescan, enrich type/default/required/enumValues/description); pure testable `param-fill-validate.ts` (`initialValues`/`validateParamValues`/`toVariableValues`).
- **Verify:** cortex `bun test` 342/0, typecheck clean, live smoke 3/3 (resolve substitutes / `secret.` unresolved / runs 400). **KNOWN PHASE-1 GAPS (left intentional):** "save & run" path (`POST /api/agents` `runNow:true`) NOT modal-gated ‚Üí server 400s on unresolved (no fill UX yet); sweep (multi-value matrix runs) is Phase 2 (schema-ready, not built); secret store is a sibling spec. MERGED to main + RELEASED in v0.11.2 (2026-06-10); leftover branch deleted (25/26 commits patch-equivalent).

## ‚Ė∂‚Ė∂ TOOL-CALLING ROUTING REGRESSION ‚ÄĒ STAGE A FIXED (2026-06-03)
Branch `fix/text-parse-bare-toolcall` (off `main` @ `152b6e59`). Symptom: "all agents fully regressing ‚ÄĒ repeat over and over, never call tools." Two faces, one root: (1) loop to max_iterations; (2) raw `<tool_call>` XML rendered as the answer.
- **Root cause (trace-verified):** `482c11e4` keyed the tool-call DRIVER on `calibration.toolCallDialect` but left the RESOLVER injection keyed on `caps.supportsToolCalling`. Ollama hardcodes `supportsToolCalling:true` for EVERY model (`local.ts:951`), so every *uncalibrated* Ollama model got NativeFCStrategy resolver (`runner.ts:126`) + TextParseDriver (`mode:text-parse`). No native tools sent (`think.ts:503`); model emits the `<tool_call>` XML the driver instructs; resolver (parses only native-FC/fenced-JSON/pseudo-code) can't read it ‚Üí `think.ts:852` resolver branch classifies thinking/final_answer and RETURNS. `TextParseDriver.extractCalls` (`act.ts:164`) is unreachable ‚ÄĒ kernel runs `handleActing` only on `status:"acting"`, which `think.ts` sets ONLY on its 2 native-FC paths (`:952`,`:1198`).
- **Deeper finding:** text-parse mode was NEVER a live path ‚ÄĒ no calibration produces the `"text-parse"` dialect (`calibration-runner` emits `none`/`native-fc`); pre-482c11e4 every model ‚Üí NativeFCDriver. `482c11e4` switched on a half-built path (no think‚Üíacting transition for text markup).
- **Stage A fix (`11996c5a`):** capability is the single master signal. `selectToolCallingDriver(dialect, supportsToolCalling)` ‚Üí native unless `supportsToolCalling===false`. `runner.ts` resolves caps ONCE, feeds both resolver injection + driver selection ‚Üí coherent triple (injectResolver ‚üļ native driver ‚üļ attachTools). Verified gemma4:e4b 0-call/21-iter/13k ‚Üí file-write+final-answer/6-step/4.6k/success (N=3 3/3); cogito:14b (482c11e4's trigger) fixed. tools 819 / reasoning 1576 / runtime 907 green. Direct worktree fix (pilot override).
- **Boundary:** tool-INCAPABLE Ollama models (gemma3:12b ‚Üí `/api/chat` `"does not support tools"`) now fail fast+loud (`llm_error`, 1.4s, 0 tok) vs 482c11e4's silent 13k-tok loop ‚ÄĒ net-positive, still can't use tools.
- **Stage B (NOT started):** narrow `local.ts:951` to per-model `/api/show` tools probe **COUPLED WITH** building the text-parse think‚Üíacting transition (detect `<tool_call>` ‚Üí `pendingNativeToolCalls`+`status:acting`; driver pure-extraction, think.ts owns classification). Then retire older `tool-calling/resolver.ts`. Must land together or cogito trades one break for another. **[SUPERSEDED 2026-06-04 ‚ÄĒ Stage B subsumed by the calibration-adapter design at ¬ß"WEAK-MODEL TOOL-CALL GAP" below; not a standalone next-step.]**
- Spec `wiki/Architecture/Design-Specs/2026-06-03-tool-calling-driver-redesign.md`; evidence `wiki/Research/Harness-Reports/2026-06-03-tool-calling-routing-n3.md`; register R1(closed)/R2(open). No cloud keys in env ‚Üí cross-tier cloud gate deferred.
